[30;1m478 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m479 | [0m[35mIf you wish to use e.g. `gunicorn` or `waitress` to deploy the dashboard you should add [0m
[30;1m480 | [0m[35m`app = db.flask_server()` to your code to expose the Flask server. You can then [0m
[30;1m481 | [0m[35mstart the server with e.g. `gunicorn dashboard:app` [0m
[30;1m482 | [0m[35m(assuming the file you defined the dashboard in was called `dashboard.py`). [0m
